we are marking National Day for Truth and Reconciliation at Kunitz Shoes.\\n\\n10\u0025 of all proceeds from sales at our stores today will be donated to Legacy of Hope Foundation.\\n\\nWe've operated for over 40 years on Treaty 6 land and acknowledge that we are on traditional territories of the many First Nations, M\u00e9tis, and Inuit in Alberta and express gratitude and respect for the land we use, and have committed to advancing reconciliation.\\n\\nAs a family and as business owners, the Kunitz Family is working towards finding our place in reconciliation. We respect that each person will experience reconciliation in their own way, and for our part we have chosen to move towards action where possible.\\n\\nOur first actions on this front will be on display in an upcoming Indigenous-led collaboration collection. Throughout the concept and design phase of this project we\u2019ve been working and learning with local Indigenous designers and community leaders. A part of the sales proceeds from the collection will be donated to one or more grassroots organizations focused on Survivor assistance right here in Edmonton. \\n\\nThe results of the project are stunning, artistic, political and at times uncomfortable- it will raise more questions than answers, and we feel that this is what makes the project such an important part of our reconciliation journey.\\n.\\n.\\n.\\n.\\n#truthandreconciliationday #orangeshirtday
